 Other party leaders were present at the time of the announcement, but the former Deputy Prime Minister did not appear before the media
 adwani ke tevar main narmi aresas ke pramukh mohan bhagwat ke samajhane ke baad ai
 Bhagwat urged him to withdraw his decision to leave the National Executive, Parliamentary Board and Election Committee
 rajnath singh ne bataaya, "aaj dopaher mohan bhagwat ne adwaniji se baat kii or unase rashtrahit main party padon par bane rahane ke liye kaha
 "he continued," Advani has decided to accept Bhagwatji's advice
 " Rajnath Singh's statement is a pseudo-confirmation that the BJP failed to convince Advani after he resigned all the posts of the party, resenting his concerns in nominating Narendra Modi as the head of the election campaign committee
 He collaborated with Atal Bihari Vajpayee and other leaders in 1980
 adwani ke party padon se istipha dene or party ke adhikansh netaaon par nijee agenda ko tarjeeh dene kaa aarope lagane ke baad bhaajapa ke bade netaaon ne unke awaas par deraa daal diya, lekin ve tus se mas nahin hue
 Rajnath Singh announced on Monday that Advani's resignation from the party's posts would not be accepted
 mangalvaar ko bhaajapa netaaon or adwani kii baithak jari rahi
 Many leaders had emphasized that this crisis will be resolved soon
 modi ke mukhar samarthakon main se ek rajnath singh ne kaha, "party kii taraf se maine adwaniji ko aashwast kiya he ki party ke kaamkaaj ke sambandh main unki chintaaon kaa samaadhaan kiya jayega or main unke saath un chintaaon ke samaadhaan kii yukti par charchaa karunga
 " bhaajapa adhyaksh ke saath sushamaa swaraj, nitin gadakari or uma bharti ke alaava anya varisht netaa maujuud the
 Advani stayed away from the national executive meeting as an excuse for illness
 sampurna raajnneetik jivan main yah pehla mauka tha jab adwani bhaajapa kii ek mahatvapurn baithak se alag rahe
 At the time when the entire party was busy celebrating Modi's elevation, Advani resigned and shocked everyone
 istife se bhi zyada bhaajapa ko adwani ke istife ke patr main lagaaya gaya yah aarope ki 'yah adarshavaadi party nahin rahi' ne aahat kiya tha
 He also said that he was finding himself unable to keep pace with the bjp's current functioning or the direction it was going
 yadhyapi modi party ke aam sadasyon ke bich lokapriy netaa ho chuke hai phir bhi bhaajapa kii kai pradesh ikaiyaan samet ek bada varg adwani ke saath sahanubhuti rakhata he
 Advani and Vajpayee remained the faces of the Jan Sangh and later its successor BJP for decades
 tippaniyan After the end of the crisis, Shahnawaz Hussain said on Tuesday, "he has played a big role in making the party stand and it is hoped that his blessings will remain
" " The National Democratic Alliance (NDA), which is running in distress from the crisis within the BJP, also breathed a sigh of relief
 bhaajapa kii sahyogi or rajg kii ghatak janata dal-united ke kasee tyaagi ne kaha ki rajg ventilator par tha or use adwani se oxygen kii ummid thi
 The decision regarding Advani was announced by party president Rajnath Singh at his residence
 ghoshnaa ke samay party ke anya netaa to maujuud the, lekin purv up pradhanmantri media ke saamne nahin aae
 The softness in Advani's tone came after RSS chief Mohan Bhagwat explained
 bhagwat ne unase rashtriya kaaryakarini, sansadeey board or chunaav samiti chhodane kaa apana faisla waapas lene kaa aagrah kiya
 Rajnath Singh told, "this afternoon Mohan Bhagwat spoke to Advaniji and asked him to hold party posts in the national interest
 " unhone aage kaha, "adwaniji ne bhagwatji kaa paraamarsh sweekaar karne kaa faisla liya he
 " rajnath singh kaa bayaan is baat kii chhadam pushti he ki narendra modi ko chunaav prachaar samiti kaa pramukh namit kiye jane main apni chintaaon ko darkinar kiye jane se naaraaz hokar party ke sabhi padon istipha dene ke baad vahi bhaajapa adwani ko manaane main naakaam rahi jisaki sthapana unhone 1980 main atal bihari vaajapeyi va anya netaaon ke saath milakar kii thi
 After Advani resigned from party posts and accused most of the party leaders of preferring personal agenda, senior BJP leaders camped at his residence, but they did not budge
 rajnath singh ne somvaar ko ghoshnaa kii thi ki adwani kaa party ke padon se istipha manjuur nahin kiya jayega
 The meeting of BJP leaders and Advani continued on mangalvaar ko bhaajapa netaaon or adwani kii baithak jari rahi
 Many leaders had emphasized that this crisis will be resolved soon

 At the time when the entire party was busy celebrating Modi's elevation, Advani resigned and shocked everyone
 istife se bhi zyada bhaajapa ko adwani ke istife ke patr main lagaaya gaya yah aarope ki 'yah adarshavaadi party nahin rahi' ne aahat kiya tha
 He also said that he was finding himself unable to keep pace with the bjp's current functioning or the direction it was going
 yadhyapi modi party ke aam sadasyon ke bich lokapriy netaa ho chuke hai phir bhi bhaajapa kii kai pradesh ikaiyaan samet ek bada varg adwani ke saath sahanubhuti rakhata he

" " The National Democratic Alliance (NDA), which is running in distress from the crisis within the BJP, also breathed a sigh of relief

 " The BJP president was accompanied by senior leaders besides Sushma Swaraj, Nitin Gadkari and Uma Bharti

 Pandit Makhanlal Chaturvedi was a brilliant nationalist writer, poet and prodigal journalist of modern India
 unka janm 4 april 1889 ko madhya pradesh ke hoshangabad jile main babai naamak jagah par hua tha

 For those devotees who have difficulty in chanting or chanting mantras, the best method of worship is the recitation of Chalisa
 aaie jaanate hai kya he chalisa kaa mahatv
 
 
 History and importance of Chalisa - Prayer performed in simple language is called Chalisa
 - jo ek bhakt apane bhagwaan yaa isht ko prasann karne liye karata he
 - Chalisa is usually recited to troubleshoot problems
 - ise chalisa isliye kehete hai kyonki isamen chalis line hoti hai
 - Chalisa can be read easily because it is written in simple language
 - isliye prarthana kii ye vidha bhakton main badi lokapriy hui
 - Different lines in Chalisa have different significance
 - vishesh tarah kii samasyaon main chalisa kii linon kaa vishesh prayog bhi hota he
 - Tulsidas ji's written poem is considered to be the most powerful and popular
 chalisa paath kii uttam vidhiishwar ko prasann karne kii sabase saral vidhaon main se ek he chalisa
 Be it the God of Gods or Vasudeva Shri Krishna, Mother Jagadamba or Mahabali Hanuman, a separate chalisa has been designed to please all the deities but very few know the best method of reciting the chalisa
 aaie jaanate hai ki kya he chalisa ke paath kii uttam vidhi
 
 
 - Sit in front of the picture or idol of the deity Kichalisa to be recited
 - dev pratimaa ke saamne jal se bharaa paatr rakhen
 - Then read Chalisa, it is best to recite Chalisa thrice
 - paath ke baad us jal ko prasad kii tarah grahan karen
 - Try that the time of reading chalisa is same daily
 - vishesh dashaon main yatra yaa sote samay bhi chalisa kaa paath kar sakate hai
 - Mantra chanting is better if mental
 - lekin chalisa kaa paath bol-bolkar yaa ga-gaakar karnaa uttam hoga
